< text>
This establishment is fairly new to Alondra Stater Brothers Plaza in Norwalk and I'm really happy that I stopped by. If you're a first time customer, you receive a complimentary coffee mug with their name and logo...really cute. I ordered 2 combo teriyaki bowls (beef and chicken) and they blew me and my husband away! Freshly grilled beef and chicken and the rice is really good, too. Went back tonight and ordered a fried, spicy tuna sushi roll and again, totally delicious. Oh and health board graded them an "A"....I concur, they really deserve it.
P.S. Check out their spicy chicken ramen for $6.50...loved it!</text>

<rating>2<//rating>< Review>
Unfortunately when I went to eat there my service was poor and the food just adequate for the price. The place was busy but not so busy as to forget things I ordered. The pizza was ok and made in the restaurant. I understand when waiters or waitress are busy and expect longer wait times but the place was not packed and the two of us were sitting in an easy to see spot. Service aside (and that may have been a one off) the food was of ok quality. The price for the food and the quality were just ok. The pizza sauce was  plain and the bread ok. The fact that an entire salad was never brought to the table was an interesting ommision. My partner and I thought that it was just a delay (as all the food was coming very slowly) until the waiter brought us the check. I don't plan on eating there again and would recommend you check something else out.</Review>
